dp4 r1.y, c11, r2

mov o5, c14.x

"
}

Keywords { "DIRECTIONAL" "SHADOWS_OFF" "LIGHTMAP_OFF" "DIRLIGHTMAP_OFF" "DYNAMICLIGHTMAP_OFF" "VERTEXLIGHT_ON" }

Bind "color" Color
Bind "normal" Normal
Matrix 8 [_Object2World] 3
Matrix 11 [_World2Object] 3
Matrix 4 [glstate_matrix_mvp]
Vector 17 [unity_4LightAtten0]
Vector 14 [unity_4LightPosX0]
Vector 15 [unity_4LightPosY0]
Vector 16 [unity_4LightPosZ0]
Vector 0 [unity_LightColor0]
Vector 1 [unity_LightColor1]

Vector 3 [unity_LightColor3]
Vector 20 [unity_SHBb]
Vector 19 [unity_SHBg]
Vector 18 [unity_SHBr]
Vector 21 [unity_SHC]
"vs_3_0
def c22, 0, 1, 0, 0
dcl_position v0
dcl_normal v1
dcl_color v2
dcl_position o0
dcl_texcoord o1.xyz
dcl_texcoord1 o2.xyz
dcl_color o3
dcl_texcoord2 o4.xyz
dcl_texcoord5 o5
dp4 o0.x, c4, v0
dp4 o0.y, c5, v0
dp4 o0.z, c6, v0
dp4 o0.w, c7, v0
dp4 r0.x, c8, v0
add r1, -r0.x, c14
dp4 r0.y, c9, v0
add r2, -r0.y, c15
mul r3.xyz, c12, v1.y
mad r3.xyz, c11, v1.x, r3
mad r3.xyz, c13, v1.z, r3
nrm r4.xyz, r3
mul r3, r2, r4.y
mul r2, r2, r2
mad r2, r1, r1, r2
mad r1, r1, r4.x, r3
dp4 r0.z, c10, v0
add r3, -r0.z, c16
mov o2.xyz, r0
mad r0, r3, r4.z, r1
mad r1, r3, r3, r2
rsq r2.x, r1.x
rsq r2.y, r1.y
rsq r2.z, r1.z
rsq r2.w, r1.w
mov r3.y, c22.y
mad r1, r1, c17, r3.y
mul r0, r0, r2
max r0, r0, c22.x
rcp r2.x, r1.x
rcp r2.y, r1.y
rcp r2.z, r1.z
rcp r2.w, r1.w
mul r0, r0, r2
mul r1.xyz, r0.y, c1
mad r1.xyz, c0, r0.x, r1
mad r0.xyz, c2, r0.z, r1
mad r0.xyz, c3, r0.w, r0
mul r0.w, r4.y, r4.y
mad r0.w, r4.x, r4.x, -r0.w
mul r1, r4.yzzx, r4.xyzz
mov o1.xyz, r4
dp4 r2.x, c18, r1
dp4 r2.y, c19, r1
dp4 r2.z, c20, r1
mad r1.xyz, c21, r0.w, r2
add o4.xyz, r0, r1
mov o3, v2
mov o5, c22.x

"

"vs_3_0

dcl_color v2

dp4 o0.y, c1, v0
dp4 o0.z, c2, v0

add o4.xyz, r0, -c10

mov o3, v2

"
}
